<div id="content">

    <div class="o-container">

    <p class="u-text-center">Interns come from diverse backgrounds, studying all things A to Z: Applied Physics, Biology, Business (MBA), Computer Science, Economics, English, Entertainment Technology, Ethics, Illustration, International Business, Management & Information Systems, Politics, Religion, Social Psychology, Statistics—well, A to S, but we wouldn’t turn away a kickass Zoology major!</p>
    <p class="u-text-center">Interns nab honest mentorship during their time here. We work with awesome people and sharing knowledge is part of working here. You can also expect to level up while here: you'll unlock access to classes through Riot University to level up your skills while here. You'll share your hard work with all of Riot during the Intern Science Fair, when you’ll get feedback from other Rioters and see how far your work reaches when you learn how your project affects other teams.</p>
    <p class="u-text-center">Rioters tinker and build at our no holds barred 48hr internal hackathon <a href="http://thunderdome.riotgames.com/" target="_blank">Thunderdome</a>, where you can stretch the limits of your imagination and abilities.</p>
    <div class="o-spacer"></div>

    <section class="o-section-bg o-section-bg--compact o-section-bg--solid">

        <h2 class="c-heading c-heading--light">Perks of the Program?</h2>

        <div class="o-spacer o-spacer--small"></div>

        <ul class="c-list-grid clearfix">
            <li class="c-list-grid__item">
                <h4 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-heading--left c-list-grid__title">PlayFund</h4>
                <p class="c-list-grid__description">You’ll sample a taste of this annual Rioter perk, with $150 to spend on videogames.
                    <a href="http://www.riotgames.com/articles/20121029/531/funding-riots-play" target="_blank">We use it to fuel our slavering hunger</a> to consume the newest and shiniest diversions; how you use it is up to you. Well, within reason. No matter how much you want it to, Monopoly doesn’t count. No, Matt, not even the Lord of the Rings Special Edition.</p>
                <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 25 25" class="c-list-grid__icon c-icon c-icon--arrow">
                    <title>play-arrow</title>
                    <circle class="a" cx="12.5" cy="12.5" r="12.5"/>
                    <path class="b" d="M18 13l-9 5V8z"/>
                </svg>
            </li>
            <li class="c-list-grid__item">
                <h4 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-heading--left c-list-grid__title">Housing</h4>
                <p class="c-list-grid__description">Building a community with fellow interns is part of the summer experience, so we shell out for local digs a brisk walk from our offices.</p>
                <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 25 25" class="c-list-grid__icon c-icon c-icon--arrow">

                    <path class="b" d="M18 13l-9 5V8z"/>
                </svg>
            </li>
            <li class="c-list-grid__item">
                <h4 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-heading--left c-list-grid__title">Riot University Classes</h4>
                <p class="c-list-grid__description">In addition to what you’ll learn from your team and day-to-day work, you can dive into Riot U classes and pick up some fresh leadership and self-awareness augments, or sign up for productivity coaching, professional moonsurfing tours, and more.</p>
                <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 25 25" class="c-list-grid__icon c-icon c-icon--arrow">

                <p class="c-list-grid__description">From coffee chats to lunch and learns to semi-regular mixers, there's plenty of ways to get to know your fellow Rioters.</p>

        <div class="o-grid__column o-grid__column--4-md">
            <h2 class="c-heading c-heading--left">Application Timeline</h2>
            <p>Because schools vary in their schedules so do we. Take care when applying and check application deadlines.</p>

            <a href="/riot-internships/faq" class="c-button">FAQ</a>
            <br><br>

            <p class="c-footnote">
                <span class="u-color-red">*</span>There's a record number of internship candidates this year, and we can't keep up! We want every applicant to have a good experience and get the attention they've earned, so we're temporarily shuttering internship applications for Software Engineering from January 9 until February 20.
            </p>
            <p class="c-footnote">
                Haven't applied yet but want to? Fret not! We'll be re-opening applications from February 20 until March 6.
            </p>

        <div id="tabs-1" class="c-tabs__content">
            <p>Interns work on meaty projects with real impact, like pushing code to live servers, making impressively playful splash art, and building out a micro-feedback tool. You’ll gain hands-on experience working in games. Here’s just a sample of what interns have accomplished, often in under 14 weeks:</p>

            <div class="c-slider c-slider--inner-content js-slider" data-slider-tab="1">
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-grant-w.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                    <div class="c-slider__content">
                        <div class="c-slider__header">
                            <div class="c-slider__block">

                                <div class="c-slider__profile">
                                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/profile-grant-w.png" alt="" class="c-slider__portrait">
                                    <span class="c-slider__name">Grant</span>
                                </div>

                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">2016 NA Scouting Grounds</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            For my project this summer, I helped create the NA Scouting Grounds. In November, we'll be inviting the 20 best Challenger players from the NA ranked ladder to participate in a boot camp and showcase event in front of the pro LoL teams, in an esports version of a pro league scouting combine. This event is meant to be the stepping stone for players to go from being a ranked ladder climber to a LCS star.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-alex-m.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                        <div class="c-slider__header">

                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">League Client Update</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            I worked on the League client update as a Software Engineer and got to help build the new champion select experience for draft. The client update is a huge priority for the company right now, and the champion select portion has a ton of animations with the least tolerance for error, so it's been a really challenging and rewarding experience.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-zack-e.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">Esports Research</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            I conducted audience research for the Esports Content Team which produces Team Fight Breakdown and Pocket Picks. Through a combination of survey research and YouTube analytics I was able to help the team better understand how to share the current content with a larger audience, inform current content making decisions, and provide insight into future content ideas.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>

                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">Changerous</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            I worked on Changerous, an internal tool that creates an audit trail of changes made to services running in production. Because there are so many developers with production access, and so many different services running, it can be hard to track down why something is breaking, but Changerous will provide a centralized location where all recent changes can be collected and viewed.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-greg-k.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">LCU</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            This summer I worked on the League Client Update Alpha. Our team was responsible for building the Champion Detail Pages and the Landing Page. I worked on the layout and interface for the Skins tab of the Champion Details Page and the tech that allowed teams to customize landing pages in their regions. It was very rewarding to be able to deliver this improved experience to players.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-jerry-j.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/profile-michael-a.png" alt="" class="c-slider__portrait">
                                    <span class="c-slider__name">Jerry | Mike - Computer Science</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">Insights Tech</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            We worked with the Insights Tech team to build the "real-time pipeline". Send any data to the pipeline, and we'll make sure it is stored and searchable within a second! RTP gives Riot Direct real-time visibility into every player's ping, while simultaneously processing the logs from the global fleet of LoL's platform servers. It was awesome to work on and own various parts of the highly-scalable service, from data ingestion to query performance.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            Working at Riot is really exciting, it feels soooo different to work on something you care about. This project was not at all part of the projects arranged for me, but I saw a need, so I took the lead. At Riot, the culture of challenging convention to build new things really inspires me. I was working on player segmentation and realized there was a need to automate the process to make segmentation analysis more efficient for Researchers at Riot.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-michael-s.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                            </div>

When I found out my projects would include Arcade and Baker Pantheon, I was even more psyched! From beginning to end, I was encouraged to participate in strategy discussions and make design decisions that impacted the player experience. I'll never forget directing Baker Pantheon's video, either!
                        </p>

                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            As an MBA intern for Insights Analytics, I advised two groups at Riot on their strategic needs. My primary project was equipping a newly formed team (whose mission was to develop a platform for shared services across Riot's future games) with decision-making frameworks on what opportunities and products to prioritize. I also created the foundation for a dashboard showing game health metrics for Stonehearth and how their players were interacting with the game.
                        </p>

        <span property="dc:title" content="Legal Jibber Jabber (Polish)" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>    
  
  <div class="content clearfix">
    <span class="print-link"></span><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"> <h2>
	POLITYKA RIOT GAMES NA TEMAT TWORZENIA I WYKORZYSTYWANIA FILM&Oacute;W</h2>
<p>Tw&oacute;rczo naszej spoecznoci inspiruje, informuje i zapewnia rozrywk zar&oacute;wno pracownikom Riot, jak i graczom. Chcemy oglda jak najwicej film&oacute;w, w kt&oacute;rych znajduje si jak najwicej element&oacute;w zwizanych z Riot Games i League of Legends. Ten poradnik pomoe zagwarantowa, e kady film zawierajcy nasz wasno intelektualn (tak, jak fragmenty film&oacute;w, grafiki, muzyka, dwiki oraz inna zawarto) bdzie m&oacute;g by umieszczony na YouTube, stronach ze streamami, jak own3D, lub udostpniony tobie i twoim przyjacioom. Dziki tej polityce powinnicie bez problemu uzyska wszystkie niezbdne pozwolenia od stron takich jak YouTube &ndash; oraz wiedzie, jakie filmy s naszym zdaniem w porzdku.</p>
<ul>
	<li>
		<strong>Nie dla zysku (chyba, e dopuszcza to niniejszy dokument!). Wszystkie filmu musz by publicznie dostpne i nie mona pobiera za nie opat lub blokowa do nich dostpu w inny spos&oacute;b. Co to oznacza:</strong>
		<ul>
			<li>
				Nie mona da adnej opaty, wypenienia ankiety, pobrania czego (poza samym filmem) lub wykonania innej czynnoci, aby uzyska dostp do filmu.</li>
			<li>
				Film moe zosta umieszczony na stronie, kt&oacute;ra posiada patne konta &bdquo;premium&rdquo; pod warunkiem, e film bdzie dostpny dla niepaccych uytkownik&oacute;w.</li>
			<li>
				Moecie puszcza reklamy lub streamy, kt&oacute;re nie ograniczaj dostpu uytkownik&oacute;w do filmu. Podlega to pod poniszy punkt - &bdquo;Udzielanie licencji&rdquo;.</li>
		</ul>
	</li>
</ul>
<ul>
	<li>
		<strong>Udzielanie licencji. Og&oacute;lnie rzecz biorc, nie moecie udziela licencji na uytkowanie filmu osobom trzecim za opat lub inn form wynagrodzenia, bez naszej zgody. Jednake, istnieje kilka wyjtk&oacute;w:</strong>
		<ul>
			<li>
				Programy partnerskie z YouTube lub stronami takimi jak: own3D.tv, Ustream.tv, Twitch.tv, Justin.tv, Blip.tv (nasze pozwolenie nie jest wymagane).</li>
			<li>
				Do wszystkich innych udziele licencji (takich jak festiwale filmowe, konkursy czy transmisje przez osoby trzecie), niezbdne jest udzielone przez nas pozwolenie.&nbsp;</li>
			<li>
				Wysyajcie wszystkie proby pod adres&nbsp;<a href="mailto:fansites@riotgames.com">fansites@riotgames.com</a>.</li>
		</ul>
	</li>
</ul>
<ul>
	<li>
		<strong>Sponsorowanie jest w porzdku. Jeeli chcecie wywietli logo sponsora na pocztku filmu lub podczas &bdquo;listy pac&rdquo; albo chcecie podzikowa im osobicie, to super. Kilka prostych uwag:</strong>
		<ul>
			<li>
				Wszelkie wspomnienia o sponsorach nie powinny by za dugie.</li>
			<li>
				Powiedzcie jasno (wspominajc o sponsorze lub wywietlajc napis &bdquo;sponsorowane przez&rdquo; przy ich logo), e jest to tylko i wycznie wasz sponsor.</li>
			<li>
				Nie wykorzystujcie loga Riot Games (lub League of Legends) bez naszej zgody.&nbsp;</li>
		</ul>
	</li>
</ul>
<ul>
	<li>
		<strong>Trzymajcie si tematu filmu. Absolutny zakaz stosowania rasistowskiej, seksistowskiej, homofobicznej lub w jakikolwiek spos&oacute;b obraliwej zawartoci. Chcemy take prosi, aby wasze filmy skupiay si na grach, a nie religijnych, politycznych i innych kontrowersyjnych tematach.</strong></li>
	<li>
		<strong>Szanujcie innych tw&oacute;rc&oacute;w. Poza wasnoci intelektualn Riot, nie umieszczajcie tam adnej zawartoci, kt&oacute;ra nie jest waszego autorstwa, chyba, e posiadacie zgod autora. Nie dajcie zarobi prawnikom!</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>Jeeli macie jakie pytania dotyczce tej polityki, skontaktujcie si z nami pod adresem&nbsp;<a href="mailto:fansites@riotgames.com">fansites@riotgames.com</a>.</p>

							</td>

								<b>Câncer</b>
								<p>Saia da sua zona de conforto e experimente algo totalmente diferente. Só tenha cautela para não se desentender com os filhos. A diversão e o carinho animam a convivência os amigos.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
											<tr>
							<td width="120">
								<img src="/diariosaopaulo/upload/horoscopo/99615731signo_03.jpg" border="0" alt="Capricórnio" title="Capricórnio">
							</td>
							<td>
								<b>Capricórnio</b>
								<p>Seu lado possessivo fica mais evidente. Cuide do que é seu e evite emprestar algo para um amigo. Mesmo assim, a companhia da turma tem tudo para agitar este domingo.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
											<tr>
							<td width="120">
								<img src="/diariosaopaulo/upload/horoscopo/87673872signo_02.jpg" border="0" alt="Escorpião" title="Escorpião">
							</td>
							<td>
								<b>Escorpião</b>
								<p>Você vai dedicar mais tempo aos familiares, mas é melhor se policiar para não bater de frente com alguém de casa. O diálogo é a melhor maneira de se entender com as pessoas queridas.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
											<tr>
							<td width="120">
								<img src="/diariosaopaulo/upload/horoscopo/38447169signo_09.jpg" border="0" alt="Gêmeos" title="Gêmeos">
							</td>
							<td>
								<b>Gêmeos</b>
								<p>Não deixe a saúde em segundo plano e mantenha qualquer tipo de exagero bem longe. A vontade de curtir e aproveitar intensamente a vida será grande. Viagem pode agitar o domingo.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
											<tr>
							<td width="120">
								<img src="/diariosaopaulo/upload/horoscopo/5581578signo_01.jpg" border="0" alt="Leão" title="Leão">
							</td>
							<td>
								<b>Leão</b>
								<p>Pode receber boas novas sobre a saúde de um parente. Melhor não misturar romance e família. Não aceite palpite na sua vida amorosa. Seu jeito carinhoso fica em evidência.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
											<tr>
							<td width="120">
								<img src="/diariosaopaulo/upload/horoscopo/41156850signo_04.jpg" border="0" alt="Libra" title="Libra">
							</td>
							<td>
								<b>Libra</b>
								<p>Comprar algo para o lar pode ser uma boa. Se precisa de grana emprestada, converse com um familiar. Só não gaste além da conta. Charmosa e atraente será fácil atrair e envolver quem deseja.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
											<tr>
							<td width="120">
								<img src="/diariosaopaulo/upload/horoscopo/29959797signo_07.jpg" border="0" alt="Peixes" title="Peixes">
							</td>
							<td>
								<b>Peixes</b>
								<p>Passeio com os amigos levanta seu astral e conta com a proteção das estrelas. Só fique atento a alguns imprevistos. Com jogo de cintura, dá para virar o jogo e manter o bom humor.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
											<tr>
							<td width="120">
								<img src="/diariosaopaulo/upload/horoscopo/75087512signo_11.jpg" border="0" alt="Sagitário" title="Sagitário">
							</td>
							<td>
								<b>Sagitário</b>
								<p>Pode surgir um dinheiro que não esperava, ainda mais se lidar com as finanças de maneira discreta. Seu lado inquieto vem à tona: saia de casa e deixe a mesmice bem longe.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
											<tr>
							<td width="120">
								<img src="/diariosaopaulo/upload/horoscopo/28089854signo_13.jpg" border="0" alt="Touro" title="Touro">
							</td>
							<td>
								<b>Touro</b>
								<p>Se depender dos astros, estará mais sensível ao que as outras pessoas pensam a seu respeito, por isso, é melhor pegar leve. Viagem ou contato com alguém de fora está protegido.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
											<tr>
							<td width="120">
								<img src="/diariosaopaulo/upload/horoscopo/92815321signo_08.jpg" border="0" alt="Virgem" title="Virgem">
							</td>
							<td>
								<b>Virgem</b>
								<p>Talvez precise encarar fofocas e mal-entendidos na convivência com alguns colegas. Aja com cautela e pense duas vezes antes de contar algo para pessoas que conhece superficialmente.</p>
							</td>
						</tr>
